 (* Write a function to divide two lists element wise. *)
let rec divide x y =
  match x, y with
  | [], [] -> []
  | x::xs, y::ys ->
      let x = x::xs in
      let y = y::ys in

  match x, y with

 (* Write a function to divide two lists element wise. *)
let rec divide x y =
  match x, y with
  | [], [] -> []
  | x::xs, y::ys ->
      let x = x::xs in
